**Complimentary Copy** NOT FOR SALE 

**STATISTICAL SUPPLEMENT** Pakistan Economic Survey 2017-18 

Economic Adviser’s Wing, Finance Division, Government of Pakistan, Islamabad 

## **PREFACE** 

The Statistical Supplement is published annually by the Economic Adviser’s Wing in addition to the Pakistan Economic Survey which is released prior to the presentation of the Federal Budget. The Statistical Supplement updates the information contained in the Pakistan Economic Survey for the complete fiscal year while the economic analysis and social developments in the Economic Survey is based on the data available for 8 to 9 months. Hence, the present Statistical Supplement is meant to update the statistics contained in the Pakistan Economic Survey 2017-18. 

The economic and social aggregates in the Survey are presented for the convenience of users with a maximum depth and greater intra-sectoral details. The information contained in the Statistical Supplement is also based on the input of various Ministries/Departments who timely provided the data to Economic Adviser’s Wing. Soft version of the Statistical Supplement is also available on Finance Division Web Site and on Compact Discs as well. 

Readers are welcome to provide suggestions for improvement of the Statistical Supplement. 

**(S. EJAZ WASTI)** Economic Adviser 

FINANCE DIVISION Islamabad, December 10, 2018

## **Note:** 

**1. Total Area Reported is the total physical area of the villages/deh, tehsils or districts etc.** 

**2. Forest Area is the area of any land administered as forest under any legal enactment dealing with forests. Any cultivated area which may exist within such forest is shown under heading "cultivated area".** 

**3. Area Not Available for Cultivation is that uncultivated area of the farm which is under farm home-steads, farm roads and other connected purposes and not available for cultivation.** 

**4. Culturable Waste is that uncultivated farm area which is fit for cultivation but was not cropped during the year under reference nor in the year before that.** 

**5. Current Fallow (ploughed but uncropped) is that area which is vacant during the year under reference but was sown at least once during the previous year** 

- **Cultivated Area is that area which was sown at least during the year under reference or during the previous year. Cultivated Area = Net Area sown + Current Fallow.** 

**6. Net Area Sown is that area which is sown at least once during (Kharif & Rabi) the year under reference.** 

**7. Area Sown more than once  is the difference between the total cropped area and the net area sown.** 

**8. Total Cropped Area means the aggregate area of crops raised in a farm during the year under reference including the area under fruit trees.**

**Note:** 

- ***: Note:Islamic Financing , Advances (against Murabaha etc) and other related items previously reported under other Assets has been reclassified as credit to private sector.** 

**1 : Effective from 22 July 2006, demand & time deposits have been re-classified in accordance with Banking Surveillance Department circular no. 9, 2006 dated 18 July 2006. The time deposits of less than 6 months are included in demand deposits for the purpose of Cash Reserve Requirement and Statutory Liquid Requirements.** 

**2 : Definition of time & demand liabilities as mentioned in BSD circular no 9[th] dated 18[th] July 2008 have been revised. As per new definition, time liabilities include deposits with tenor of one year and above. Accordingly, time deposits with tenor of less than one year will become part of demand deposits.**

## **WEIGHTS & MEASURES** 

## **RUPEES** 

One Lakh Ten Lakh One Crore One Billion One Trillion 

=One hundred thousand =100,000 =One million =1,000,000 =Ten million =10,000,000 =One thousand million =One thousand billion 

## **WEIGHTS** 

One Gram =0.035 Ounce =0.0857 Tola One Pound =16 ounces =453.592 grams One Kilogram =1000 grams =1.07 seers =2.205 pounds One Metric ton =1000 Kilograms =0.9842 ton =26.792 Maunds One Maund =37.3242 Kilograms One Ton =2240 pounds =1.016 metric tons One cotton bale =375 Ibs. =170.2 kg One bushel =0.73 mds =27.25 kg 

## **LENGTH** 

One yard =3 feet =36 inches =0.914 metre One mile =1760 yards =1.609 kilometres One sq. yard =0.83613 sq. metres One sq. metre =1.196 sq. yards One Acre =4840 sq. yards =0.4049 hectare One Hectare =2.47 Acres 

## **VOLUME** 

One cubic metre =35.315 cubic feet 

**LIQUID MEASURE** 

One barrel =36 imperial gallons =163.656 litres 

## **YEAR** 

FiscalYear and Agriculture Year starts from 1[st] July ends on 30[th] June Before 1959-60, the fiscal year was from April 1 to March 31 

## **CROPPING SEASONS** 

**Kharif** – Crops sown in late Spring or in the beginning of Summer and harvested in Autumn. **Rabi** – Crops sown in Autumn and harvested in the following Spring. 

Note : Indigenous system (seers, yards etc.) and Imperial system (pound, foot etc.) in Pakistan have been replaced by International system of weights and measures (kilograms, metre etc.) w.e.f. December, 1978. 

219
